Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement; et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances: c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose; donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses; si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer: lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	We have already discussed in the division the appearances of dropsy, and how the gathering of water occurs, and the signs of each appearance, and the treatment that is performed by medication, and that which is cured by iron; only [the latter] is described. One must not use iron on these two appearances: that is, tympanites and hydrops, for this is a deadly thing. Therefore, when you treat this appearance of dropsy, which is called 'eclites', with medication, and the cure does not help, then consider if the patient is weak, or has another illness other than dropsy, such as dysentery and similar conditions; one must not use iron, for there is doubt. But if you see a strong person who only has dropsy, and he is neither too young nor too old, one should proceed in this way: lift the patient straight up by your hands, and the attendant presses the belly by pushing the water to its lowest part under the foot, then take the spathulum according to this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And make an incision of 2 parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier; puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines: si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil; et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois; et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu; puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor; puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	And make an incision of 2 parts. And yet it must not be so deep that it reaches the intestines when you push it in, and it must not bleed; then check if the dropsy is on the side of the intestines: if it is due to a liver disease, then your incision should be on the left side of the abdomen 3 fingers down; and if it's due to the spleen, it should be on the right, and the patient must not lie on the incision so that the fluids do not flow to that weak spot; then pierce the skin all around with a needle, and squeeze it, and leave your hand on the whole spastic area between the skin and the syphon as you would when skinning, to the thickness of a fingernail or an inch; then pierce the syphon until the fluid comes out, and that is where the water is located, then draw it out, and insert this instrument from which the mold will come out:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus; et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus; et II d’autre part, et I d’autre; et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	And it is similar to a silver-colored wire, and is made of bronze or lightweight steel, and has in the lower part a small hole; and on one side, three holes; and two on the other, and one on the other; and the head is cut like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that the scribes make to trim the quill:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument; vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort; mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz; puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere; puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit; fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	at the top of this is the handle, so that when the instrument reaches its destination, it is drawn up to the instrument immediately; therefore empty half or a third of it, for if you empty more than is appropriate in that hour, by chance the patient may die from the shock of the instrument, or he will faint, or he will come close to death; but empty according to the quantity of his strength, and according to what the dispositions of his strength indicate, and his pulses; then withdraw the instrument and retain the water, which is now retained by the membrane that blocks the hole above the syphon, about which I have spoken, in such a way as you pierce it according to this method; then reinsert the instrument the next day if you see the patient able to endure it, and withdraw a little water; do this on one day, and be careful not to overdo it until he has no more water but just a little.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre; et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	If you doubt the disease, and you leave it with a lot of water, then cure it with a warm grave or sand, and by much sweating or bathing, and in the sun; and dye it with drink; and cure it with medicines that dry up until it is healed, and cauterize over the stomach and over the liver and over the spleen after the extraction of the fluid, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without a foreskin, or with a small foreskin, or it is not in its place.

puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close. Those who do not have an opening in their place are bleeder, for some are born with an opening at the head of the penis, which prevents them from urinating before they lift their penis upwards; and they cannot ejaculate because the material cannot reach the glans, and this is a serious illness.

des pustules de la verge	of the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes; si covient que tu les preignes a .i. oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien; puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez. The cautery has two uses: for bleeding and for corruption; and if the head of the penis is damaged and withdrawn, one must insert a lead pipe into the urethra and the patient should urinate through it; and when there is hair at the tip of the penis due to an uncircumcised person, either from a wound or an abscess, one must scrape it with a chisel-like instrument, so that the ligatures are loosened and the head of the penis is freed from all sides; and if it is a difficult thing to discuss, one should scrape it with a spatula-like instrument at the urethra and the skin; then pull gently between them, and place a thin damp linen cloth in cold water so that it does not become erect again.
de la circoncision	on circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not a matter of continuous dissection like other wounds; nevertheless, when we perform this act intentionally and properly on infants, it is necessary for us to do the best and most gentle job for their well-being.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not mention the circumcision of their children, because they did not use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experimentation.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	Because I have seen the majority of masters and surgeons who made circumcisions all around, and on many occasions, and on a single newborn; the foreskin would then heal because there were two membranes, and sometimes one would be cut above and the other remained beneath.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Now they recover by covering, and the pain is doubled, and with the cleaning which is done on the penis is not secure the tip of the member; and in the cleaning of the nail sometimes the iron slips, and ruins the work, and many times are born so that they do not need to be cleaned and I have seen it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	From the cleaning that is done on the scrotum, I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the testicles are cut justly above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues; puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens; puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens; puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien; et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge; puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Because when you press your hand, you cut evenly in I all the time; but let the thread be well stretched around the skin; and let the manner of the first work be that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are not forcing him to tie the thread around the wand only, and then make him pull it in all the ways you can; then let him stand between your hands straight, and support the forces between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them, nor any of the instruments; then put your hand on the wand and breathe on the heart, and draw it up so that the head of the wand is in; then cleanse it well from the filth that has gathered there, then tie the place marked with a double thread, then tie it under I to the other bond; and hold it by the second bond with the index finger and thumb, and press between the two bonds, then lift the heart quickly and draw the head of the wand; then let the blood run little by little, for this is the wound; and put powder on top of the powder the cloth glued with a cooked egg yolk tempered with rose water, confited with good and fresh rosemary oil, and leave it on until the next day, and cure it with another cure until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The shape of the forces at the mouthing is as follows: both sides are to be thin and sharp, and the ears should be as big as the palm of the hand equally.
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	the error of the purification is when the pus within the incision has dried up; therefore you must extend it with your fingernail so that the wound forms an abscess; and scrape it equally, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, then hold it with tweezers and scrape it.

And if it persists for 3 days, and that which is under the foreskin is swollen, then let it be until the abscesses are calm and the skin is lightly scraped; then scrape it as much as you can, and beware of the part of the foreskin, it will not harm him in any way.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point; cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore treat the area of the wound with powdered medicine, as we have said in the treatise on powders; and if one scrapes too much from the core, and it goes upward, it will not harm him; therefore cure it as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division; et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e; et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	The retention of urine is due to the presence of a stone, or frozen blood, or bowels, or birth matter, or similar things that we have described in the division. And if the urine is not released and you see that the retention is caused by the stone which is lodged at the neck of the bladder, then the patient should bend over his knees; and his feet should be placed on his back, and he should press his abdomen from above the back, and restrain himself as much as he can. This forces the neck of the bladder to express the stone upwards, causing the urine to flow. And if it does not come out as we have described, and the patient feels great pain, then you must use an instrument called a 'syringe', which has this form: it should be made of thin silver like the feathers of a bird; the tube should be about a palm and a half in length, and thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede; puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine; et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And the way of the emission of urine is that you take a double thread, and tie to the end a little wool or cotton, and put the end of the thread into the syringe; and squeeze out the superfluity of the wool and fill it up to the end of the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and egg white; and let the patient sit on a seat, and raise the bladder and the penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water; then gently put the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then tie the penis above towards the testicles; then fill the syringe up to the bladder, and feel the patient urinate until the bladder is empty, and if this is not done according to this order, because the person who leads it there is wrong; then extract the thread all the way through the wool, and the urine follows the wool, then pull it out, and let the urine flow; and repeat the syringe until the bladder is emptied and the patient relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	of diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scabs or blood comes into the bladder, or pus is accumulated there, and you see it oozing out with water and medicine, then do everything using the instrument called "clepsydra", and that is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus: II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est; et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira; et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	It is closed and has three openings: two on one side and one on the other, as you can see; and the hollow cheved where the medicine is applied should be such that it blocks the penis without addition, so that one can withdraw moisture and reinsert when necessary; and when you see your medicines moving in the bladder, place the end of the catheter into the moisture and suck out the moisture that is within; then insert the catheter firmly, and the moisture will enter inside and go to the bladder immediately, so that the patient feels it; and this is the form of the subtle catheter with which one cathesizes the bladder: thus it is:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie; et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And it is made of silver or brass, and the tip is higher up; and below there is one testicle or both testicles hanging; then take a mutton bladder and put the moisture that you want to cathesize the bladder into it, then tie it between the two testicles with a strong double string, and heat this moisture over a fire; then insert the tip of the catheter into the penis, then squeeze your hand over the bladder gently so that the moisture comes into the bladder; and if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and make a circle out of it, and pierce it all around; then tie the string firmly through these openings, then assemble the circle as one assembles a wheel, and put inside what you want of oil and moisture and water, and attach it to the instrument; and do as you did with the bladder, squeezing your hand so that the moisture comes into the bladder.
de la piere	of stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already spoken in the division of stones, and their extraction together with medicines; and I have said the difference between the stone in the testicles, and all the signs, and which type of stone one must work on in surgery; and in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will tell you plainly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that the stone which is in the bladder occurs most often in children, and it is a sign that the urine flows from the bladder like water in its subtlety; and it appears hairy, and causes pain to the patient, and they can urinate many times, and then they become constipated; and many of these have a hernia; and the healing is much easier in children until they are 4 years old, and it is much more serious in the elderly, and it is in between youth and old age, for those who are between youth and old age; and the cure is much easier in those who have large stones than in those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient through an enema, to draw out all the feces that are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes blocks the search for stones.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche dedens; se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	Then take the patient by the feet and turn him upside down so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes comes out from above; then let him sit between your hands with his hands under his thighs so that the bladder is completely tilted downward; then probe and feel around inside it; if you feel the stone in the space, then hurry and cut on the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	And if it does not come out with touching from the top, then wet your index finger of your left hand with oil, if the patient is old, or with your middle finger, if the patient is an adolescent; and insert it into his anus, and probe for the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, push it toward the neck of the bladder; then press on your finger, and draw it out to where you want to cut.Et s’ele ne chiet pas al col de la vessie, si lache ton doi et ta main, et quier a nouel entree le col de la vessie; et s’ele descende au parfond, si quier la piere dedens, et s’ele ne se moue point sus li col, si quier al costez; et s’ele chiet a l’espaice, si taille sus l’espaice qui est entre le col et la piere.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And instruct the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and instruct the patient to extend his testicles upward with his right hand, and with his left hand pull back the skin underneath the testicles in the area where the incision is made; then insert the spatulum, which has a curved shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans; par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And they cut between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the navel; and let it be straight on the stone, and both fingers be on the anus, and let the incision be diagonal so that it is wide at the top and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large; perhaps it presses so much on the finger which is in the anus that it comes out without effort; and know that there is a kind of stone where there are angles and edges: this is difficult to extract; and there is a kind that is below, similar to a grape, and round, whose extraction is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole; et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	And for that kind where there are angles and edges, make the incision larger; and if it does not come out, you must grip it with pincers which are like a file at the tip, to pull out the stone so that it does not escape; or you insert under it an instrument with a curved tip; and if you cannot grab it thus, then widen the opening and, if there is bleeding, stop it with vitriol; and if there is more than one stone, first insert the largest at the neck of the bladder, then push upwards, then pull it out, and finally the smaller ones.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it needs to be sutured, and a larger wound made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces; et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	For two things can happen to the patient: either they die, or the urine comes out through the wound that cannot heal; but nevertheless, keep pulling with tweezers, until you have pulled it out in pieces; and when you have finished your work, then dress the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and compress it, and put a wet cloth on top soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess; then re-bind the scrotum to the body, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, wash the site well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit; puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And if hot abscesses and corrosions and congealed blood come in the wound and the urine is retained, which is known in such a way that it comes out with the urine: then pierce your finger in the wound, and draw out that blood, for if it remains, it will corrupt the bladder and burst; then wash the wound with water and vinegar and salt, and aid him in every way you know how, until he is healed; and it is necessary that each hour that you treat him, you tie his two thighs together, and assemble the remedies on the spot.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	And if the stone is small, and it is in the passage of the penis, and lodged there, and the urine cannot pass; then the cure of what I have said before, that you cut it many times, is an excuse for not cutting it with this cure.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have tried this myself.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take a piece of iron according to this shape and let it be spiked at three angles on a poker:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone so that it cannot go back into the bladder; then push the needle into the penis gently, until it reaches the stone; and turn the needle in your hand inside the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone from another side; then the urine will come out at once, then press your hand on what is left of the stone that is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides; et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it is broken at once, and comes out with the urine, then the patient is cured; and if you cannot do this for any reason that causes pain, then tie a thread below the stone and another above, then cut the penis between the two threads, then pull the stone out, and untie the thread and cleanse the congealed blood in the wound; and treat it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of women's stones
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It sometimes happens that a stone becomes lodged in a woman's body, and if it does, the cure is difficult, and is forbidden for three reasons: one is that the woman might be a virgin; the second is that one cannot find a skilled woman who will submit to examination, especially if she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere; et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And the third way is that by chance one cannot find a woman who is skilled in this art of medicine; and the fourth way is that the stone of the woman is more embedded than that of a man, so it requires a deeper incision, and there is great fear involved. And if necessity arises, one should take a needle and pierce it, and if one cannot find a needle, then one should use a very fine castor's hair; and one should present a small mirror to the woman, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to do what you command in the examination of the stone. And be sure to look carefully whether the woman is a virgin: then she must press her thumb into the vagina and seek out the stone; and if she finds it, she must hold it under her thumb, and one must urge her to press her left hand firmly over the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite; puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	If you find it, you should move it gradually from the entrance of the bladder to below, until it reaches the root of the thigh; then press on the stone at the root of the thigh towards the middle of the groin, where the muscle is moved; and feel the stone in that part; and do not move your finger above or below the stone, and let the incision be small at first; then enlarge the wound if you feel the stone as sharp as the wound so that the stone can come out, and know that there are many kinds of stones: namely, small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and those with bumps.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	And if you know their appearances to identify the exit.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre; et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood comes out, put ground vitriol on it and hold it for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your work so that the stone can come out, and have the tools I told you about when extracting a stone from men to aid you in your task; and if the blood comes out and it is from the artery that has been cut, put the powder on the site and tightly apply bandages and bands, and do not re-open it, and leave the stone and don't pull it out, or the patient may die; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the swelling has gone down, return to your work until the stone is out.
de hernie carnouse	of flesh hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Aquous membrane is nothing else than an accumulation of moisture or white pus, which is found under the heart of the testicles, and which contains the egg; and it is called "pus", and sometimes it is properly located in the membrane of the egg, if one believes that it is another egg; and what happens is not known for certain.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this disease is due to weakness that comes from the testicles, and this matter is spread out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus; et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colors: or it is a jaundice color, or red, or black, or watery white, and this happens more; and these are the signs of recognizing this condition, for if it is in the white syphilis that we have mentioned, then the abscesses are ripe, a little long like the shape of an egg, and do not open the testicles, because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef; et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if there is moisture in the skin itself, then the abscesses are ripe with a part of an egg, and because of this one thinks it is another egg; and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white syphilis, then one feels it well. Therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, test all over the scrotum, from which the shape is described earlier.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, then, which comes after the instrument, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz; puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions; puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir; puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue; et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when we treat it with fire, the patient should be healed according to his strength and the fullness of his body; then he should lie on his back on something slightly raised, and have a lot of covers under him; then sit on his left side, and instruct the assistant to sit on his right, and extend the arm to one of the two ribs below the heart of the armpit; then take the spatulum, and cut the skin of the armpit between them from top to bottom, and make a straight incision through the skin of the armpit up to the white skin, and cut it carefully according to its strength; then pierce the cyst with a large needle full of water, and draw out all the water, and then place your fingers on it, and let the cyst swell upwards; and do not touch the heart of the armpit, but only the cyst; then carefully cut around the edge of the cyst, so that if you do not cut it well enough, the water will return. And if the egg has jumped out during the operation, return it to its place when you have finished operating on the cyst; then sew together the two lips of the armpit with a single stitch, and then cure it like other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the testicle corrupted by another disease, then you must tie off the vessels that are suspended, fearing a rupture of blood; then cut open the scrotum all around the suspenders, extract the testicle, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset; et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	And if the wound is split into two parts together, know that they are two branches; then you grip the other part as you did the first equally, then wipe away the blood, and put on the wound soft lamb's wool in rose oil; and put on another soft lamb's wool in wine and oil, and place it over the two branches, and place doubled cloth on top, and tie it onto all the ligament which is according to this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier; et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers; si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take two pieces of cloth, and stuff them with lamb's wool according to this form and they are sewn together at the crotch of the breeches, and one of the heads is pressed onto the buttocks up to the back, and the other on the part of the groin; and the two other heads above the two angles, and all the restraint is tied in the loop of the breeches; and sometimes this branch is medicated with cautery instead of iron, and it is that you grip the thin knife cautery, and grasp the skin of the branches, and it is scorched as we have said so that the white fluid containing the water is uncovered; then take the cautery according to this form, and pierce the white fluid at the joints, and scorch it with this thin hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille; et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And take off the bandages in every way you can, as much as you can; and be careful that the fire does not touch the egg; and know that this work is safer; and move carefully to prevent blood from flowing, and to avoid injuries caused by surgery; and if anything contradicts what you do, whether it's an abscess, bleeding, or something else, then cure what contradicts your actions, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit; pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer; puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee; et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this treatment because of its horror, then administer puncturing as I told you, and when you are certain from the signs that we have discussed that the watery fluid has stopped flowing, then let the patient sit on a high seat; then pierce the abscess in the part below up to the whole of the spatumile, and place the puncturing deep within the body; make the holes wide so that all the fluid can flow out; then put cotton over the area, and bandage it, and leave it to drain the remaining fluid, and then treat the wound until it heals; and if the white tissue does not let the fluid flow out of the wound, then you must insert a pen or the instrument used to treat dropsy patients, of which the shape is described earlier; and widen the wound, and know that the fluid will return, and will assemble again after six months or so, and when it has assembled as before, and thus the patient will pass their days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse; et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	Know that in the dissection of this vein there is fear in many dispositions, because of which I think it better to leave it; and I will tell you the work and the appearances of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I say then that many abscesses come in the body, especially in the testes; and it is due to various causes.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion; et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief; et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	This is to be known by an excess of bile and phlegm, which are spread to the bowels, or from a blow; and the color of the abscess follows the color of the body; and it causes no pain, and is a serious abscess; and sometimes there are gray, fearful, and bloody abscesses, with a flowing color, and occasionally they come from a blood vessel, or from inflammation of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois; et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	When it is from a blood vessel, it is known by the warm disposition of the abscess when you press it with your fingers; and you must not touch it.Quant il vient de voine enflee, il est conus par la color qui est fuxee, et si ne tu i touches, ne t’en approches mie tant qu’il ne soit venuz a lor nassance.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars; et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	Those who are swollen in the vein are known by their appearance and the feeling of the fingers, and anyone can well judge the size from this appearance and from other marks; and you should press the heart of the testicles, then the egg is on top, and the white membrane is drawn away from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope; et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	If the egg is already cooked with these new marks, then you must draw the egg and cut it; and if there is air in the membrane, or in what is inside the vessels, then you must release all that membrane and cut it roundly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the tumor is in the back, then you must cut it out entirely and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is finished, then dress the wound with wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then apply other remedies until it is healed.Et quant tu as curé la plaie, si covient que li patient soit a l’ombrage et au repos, et qu’il s’alimente de boire et manger legier, et qu’il ait peu de dormance, si com il oult.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait; et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	This is an abscess wrapped in a wrapper similar to a berry, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient grieves greatly when he moves; and the cure for this disease is also as fearful as the one before, and yet we will tell you the treatment of it according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment; puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples; puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief; puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues; puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions; car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz; si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	Let the patient sit on an elevated seat, then tie the suspensory band of testicles tightly with your fingers, covering all the vessels near the penis, and constrict them strongly; then cut through the vessels with a sharp spatula, exposing them, and then cauterize each one, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries in the temples; then insert a needle with a double thread where the vein first appeared, and tie it to the other end; then draw them gently along the middle, according to the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted moisture; then treat the wound as in the others, or use bowels, so that any vessel that supplies the testicles is not cut; for this does no harm, and if a vein comes from all the vessels, then draw the testicles from all the vessels so that the ureter loses its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	from the root of the eye socket
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions; et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses; et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement; et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	The causes of this hernia are either from the inguinal canal, or from the extension over the abdomen in the region of the groin, causing the intestines to descend from that opening to one of the testicles; and this opening is either in the groin, or from the extension of it, and these two types of hernias come about for many reasons: from a blow, or from jumping, or from lifting a heavy load, or from straining while defecating, and from similar activities. The sign that it is from an extension of the groin is that it develops gradually over a long time, and does not appear suddenly; and the abscesses are even all the way to the bottom, because the inguinal canal presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it is a dissection of the shoulder, that it brings sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses are diverse appearances under the skin near the surface, and this is due to the output of the intestine and the body being pushed by the shoulder.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the nerves go with the intestine, and are retained inside, and cause great pain for the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these cures of iron, one must fear, for which one must avoid it.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir; puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes; puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc; puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir; puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars; puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille; et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement; et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz; puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz; puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars; puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne; et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi; et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant; puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	And the manner of the treatment is that you instruct the patient to draw up the intestine with your hand into the wound, if he can; then hold the scrotum between your hands and lift the buttocks; then the anus is on top, and pull all the skin of the testicles down from the long side; then insert a hook into the incision in the abdomen according to what you need to open the wound, and make it such that the urethra can come out; then scrape off the inguinal hernia that is under the skin of the testicles, until the hard white hernia is exposed all over; then put your index finger into what follows the testicle, between the white hernia which is under the skin of the egg, and between the second hernia, and separate what is behind the egg, and between the second hernia; and move with your right hand into the scrotum, and hold the white hernia up to your left hand, and lift the egg all the way up to the hernia; then instruct the assistant to push the egg upward, and release what is behind the ligature; then feel with your fingers if there is any intestine wrapped around the hard white hernia, and if you find anything, pull it into the abdomen; then take a needle that has a thick thread made of 10 strands, and insert it into the back part of the hernia, which is after the skin of the testicles; then grasp the ends of the threads that appear, so that there are 4 threads; then tie them together in a cross shape, and bind the hernia that we have said is under the skin of the testicles with a strong ligature of two parts; then wrap the thread around the hernia, and tie it tightly in two places, so that none of the vessels that nourish it can enter, lest an abscess form there; then put the ligature back according to the first long ligature for two fingers of that one, and after these two ligatures leave a gap of a finger’s width in the hernia that is under the skin of the testicles; then grasp the part that is under the skin of the testicles, so that the blood vessels are cut off, as we have said before; then apply moist wool soaked in oil into the wound, and apply the ligature that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilis that we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision out of fear of bloodletting.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece; puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	For this often happens, and let the ligature remain until it cuts through; and if it is slow to fall out, then use a hot iron, and place what we have said over the area until it falls out; then heal the wound with another healing method until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of flesh hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this section, I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz; puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez. Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres; et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent; et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert; et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere: et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois; et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac; et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre; puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines; puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Sometimes the rupture occurs in the veins, as we have said, and the opening appears; and no intestines come out through it, and if they do, it is very little, and one should repair it every hour; and even if he remains too long in this state, he believes that the wound or the hernia will increase in size, because of the extension of the hernia which is in the veins, as we have said, for it is extended, then becomes soft and swollen, and the opening appears; and its cure is by cautery, as we have previously said; and sometimes it is cured by iron in this way: and one should let the patient lie on his back between your hands, then apply the large salt according to the amount of three times, and then extract the hernia which is under the skin that the sweat comes from, then take the thread and place it over the visible spot of the hernia; and press it against the lower abdomen, then cut the two visible spots of the hernia on the top of the thread, and cut one and the other; then pull out the top of the thread, and do not cover the hernia or stretch anything, as I have made you aware in the cure of the rupture of the intestines; then heal it with the healing of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, clean and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The ulcer is constrained and has no appearance in the roux, and cautery is more beneficial in this case and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the testicles becomes soft in some men due to the organs within becoming softened, and it is milky white in appearance; and when one wishes to treat this, he must make the patient lie on his back, and cut the softened skin above the natural membrane; then bring together the two edges of the wound at a single stitch, or at three or four stitches tightly; then cut between the stitches, and treat it as you would other wounds until it is healed, then remove the sutures.
dou chastrement	of chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	You should know that castration is prohibited in our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to discuss it in this book. It is only necessary in two ways: the first is so that the vets can answer questions and know how to treat injuries; the second is because we often need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as bulls, rams, horses, and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	I say therefore that castration is done in two ways: by tying, or by slitting.Si tu veis chastrer bouc, et mouton, et chevaus, et bestes autres, il covient que li testicules soit atraites et alons.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	In that which we do by attraction, let us sit the beast in warm water until their joints are softened and relaxed; then pull with your hand until they are reset and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Of the castration of the testicles: you should dye the beast and press the skin of the testicles in your left hand, then tie the scrotum, and stroke each testicle a hundred times when you have thoroughly scratched them; and leave some poultice of saffron and the fine saffron which is on the vessels; and this kind of castration is better than that which is done by attraction, because with atraction something of the testicles may remain, causing the beast to desire lust; then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Of Hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	Hermaphroditism is of two kinds in men: one is that between the testicles appears also as the shape of a woman's nature, having hair, and sometimes it urinates from it; the other kind, which is rarer, is where the man has both male and female sexual organs.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other method is for women; it has a handle like a rod and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	And the treatment for men and women is that you cut off the scrotum, and treat it like any other wound; in the second method, for men whose urine exits through the skin of the testicles, there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	of the testicles
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	A hernia is a swelling in the groin, as large and ugly-looking as a hand; some women have them as large as a hand, and that is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	You should dye the excess of the hernia with your hand or fingernails, and cut it gently; and do not go too deep, lest bleeding ensues, then treat it with another treatment until it heals; and for another swelling that arises at the mouth of the vagina, use it, and perhaps it will burst, and is like a cow's udder, and so they call it in Old French "maladie kowee".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you must treat it, as we have said regarding the tenting, and heal it until it is cured.
de erratique	of the erratics
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	It is errant when the nature of the woman is not perceived, or the opening is small; and it is natural from birth, or accidental due to illness that comes to it; or it is caused by a wound, or a subtle or thick cyst, and is formed deeply in the body, or on the sides, or underneath, or wherever; and they should understand conception and childbirth, and perhaps flowers to have; and the knowledge of this is through the observation of the midwife.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the stumps are visibly close by, then cut them with your fingers or with a knife.Si li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	If it is a subtle cyst and it is close to the lips, then cut them thus: place your two index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread; then form the lips, so that the subtle cyst is cut through, and cover the stumps with the cyst; then take wool, moisten it in oil, and place it over the wound, and let the woman rest at home for several days so that it may not close up.Si li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the syphilitic sore is hard and thick, then you should cut it with a spatula similar to a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the swelling is of fresh flesh, then cut it and scrape it; and have blood-staunching medicines, such as aconite, dragon's blood, incense, and egg white; then apply a large piece of wool, so that the wound does not close; and so for a long time, and then apply a tent of dry linen; then treat with other treatments until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when there is fresh flesh in the ulcer, it should be cut in this way, unless it is a deep abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For one must not touch an abscess that is deep in the ulcer.Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins from which blood flows without control, and when hemorrhoids are old, they become throbbin; and we have already described their appearances, signs, and I will now describe those that can be cured.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and throbbin, when they are deeply embedded in the rectum, and do not appear to the touch, are not cured by a cautery with iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the mouth of the rectum, which one can feel, are those that can be cured.Si on appert li thelul et les emorroides par grant dolur, si convient que l’on le cuie par fer; car la piere n’est mie trove a la guaine, ains est trove en la chair, ou il avient grant dolor, et s’eleve li sang.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	It is necessary, therefore, to place the woman in a cold room, then heat the tongs and the comb at its roots, and then powder with medicines that constrict blood, such as aconite and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things; then bandage her feet to the wall for an hour, then put her in cold water; and if bleeding occurs, have her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate bark and gallnuts and similar things, and then take barley flour, and cook it with honey and garlic, and make a plaster of it on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	And if not, have her breathe in bellows on the back and on the breasts without bleeding; then take wool, and moisten it in plantain juice or in dogwood juice with old wine, and have it breathed in at the affected spot.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the abscess has settled, treat it with ointment until it is healed; and that which is called "albathir" is red, and resembles rough ash, so it should be covered as I have said [before]; and then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	of abscesses in the rectum
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscesses come about in the body, such as ulcers and pus-filled sores, and herpes, and boils, and fistulas, and hemorrhoids, and hot abscesses, and various other ailments which I have detailed in the classification.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	Therefore, I should explain in this treatise about the hot abscess that arises in the body, which is not among the abscesses that are found in the bowels; and if you wish to know its treatment, observe whether the abscess is sharp at the beginning of its appearance, and filled with heat and fever, and turns red when you can see it.
